## Integrating with Salesforce OpenSDK 

Welcome to the Salesforce OpenSDK documentation. OpenSDKs provides a type-safe and standardized way to interact with various APIs, ensuring a consistent and efficient integration experience.

The Salesforce OpenSDK allows you to easily integrate with the Salesforce API, providing a robust set of tools to manage your API interactions with managed auth by OpenInt.

| **GET** | /sobjects/{sObject}/deleted | 
| **DESCRIPTION** | /sobjects/{sObject}/describe | 
| **GET** | /sobjects/{sObject}/describe | 
| **GET** | /sobjects/{sObject}/{id}/{blobField} | 


## Code Example

```typescript

    import {initSDK} from '@opensdks/runtime'
    import {salesforceSdkDef} from '@opensdks/sdk-salesforce'

    const salesforce = initSDK(salesforceSdkDef, {
      auth: {
        // for provider-specific auth
        bearer: `${process.env['SALESFORCE_TOKEN']}`,
        // or for passthrough auth via OPENINT_API_KEY & end user resourceId
        openInt: {
          apiKey: `${process.env['OPENINT_API_KEY']}`,
          resourceId: END_USER_RESOURCE_ID,
        }
      }
    })

    
    const res = await salesforce.DESCRIPTION('/sobjects')
```
